          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;

        }

          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;

          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

          padding: 0.5em 16px;

        }

          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

1. Start Chrome with PoC.html. e.g. chrome

DevTools: Fix UaF with portal activation

<br>



<br>





There is a slight gap between when the DevToolsUIBindings object is destroyed and when the DevToolsWindow is cleaned up. We currently would



<span class="line"><!---->There is a slight gap between when the DevToolsUIBindings object is destroyed and when the DevToolsWindow is cleaned up. We currently would<!----></span>



<br>





execute the reattach callback in the destructor, which would then go on



<span class="line"><!---->execute the reattach callback in the destructor, which would then go on<!----></span>



<br>





to access the bindings of the window that is being destroyed (hence the UAF).



<span class="line"><!---->to access the bindings of the window that is being destroyed (hence the UAF).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This patch moves the reattach callback to be run after we remove the



<span class="line"><!---->This patch moves the reattach callback to be run after we remove the<!----></span>



<br>





window is removed from the global list of instances (so it won't be



<span class="line"><!---->window is removed from the global list of instances (so it won't be<!----></span>



<br>





retrieved by the callback).



<span class="line"><!---->retrieved by the callback).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. <a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1158376" title="Security: Browser process heap-use-after-free in the portal element"><!---->issue 1158376<!----></a>

<br>



<br>





The change in reward amounts around non-web accessible security issues is not specific issues in the Portals feature, but to all Chrome bugs. In February 2022, we updated the Chrome VRP rules and policies [1] to communicate lower reward amounts for security bugs that are harder to exploit and more difficult for the attacker to successfully use. This update was also communicated directly to the Chrome VRP researcher community via email. 



<span class="line"><!---->The change in reward amounts around non-web accessible security issues is not specific issues in the Portals feature, but to all Chrome bugs. In February 2022, we updated the Chrome VRP rules and policies [1] to communicate lower reward amounts for security bugs that are harder to exploit and more difficult for the attacker to successfully use. This update was also communicated directly to the Chrome VRP researcher community via email. <!----></span>



<br>





"The amounts listed are for good quality reports that don't require complex or unlikely user interaction. Reports of issues that rely heavily or solely on user interaction, instead of being triggered by remote content, will generally receive significantly reduced rewards. Less convincing or more constrained bug submissions will likely qualify for reduced reward amounts, as chosen at the discretion of the reward panel."



<span class="line"><!---->"The amounts listed are for good quality reports that don't require complex or unlikely user interaction. Reports of issues that rely heavily or solely on user interaction, instead of being triggered by remote content, will generally receive significantly reduced rewards. Less convincing or more constrained bug submissions will likely qualify for reduced reward amounts, as chosen at the discretion of the reward panel."<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





We will be updating our rules and policies further in the near future (as well as communicating those updates to the researcher community) to add further clarity and information around reward amounts and reward decision criteria. 



<span class="line"><!---->We will be updating our rules and policies further in the near future (as well as communicating those updates to the researcher community) to add further clarity and information around reward amounts and reward decision criteria. <!----></span>



<br>

          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
